if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != '7e15c6824e74072ee90d417e2141d6e655e1c9a7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '7e15c6824e74072ee90d417e2141d6e655e1c9a7') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'ac09672e4100dba21d05ef88487f991812358e77') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '7e15c6824e74072ee90d417e2141d6e655e1c9a7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '9ba682b77d2d9a0fc3726a8be2c2de2f9de0b23e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '9ba682b77d2d9a0fc3726a8be2c2de2f9de0b23e') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '50bfff256afa3b8f972333da624a497b943cd1b7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '9ba682b77d2d9a0fc3726a8be2c2de2f9de0b23e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') != 'a7343bdb0615881e3bf900bfaf42eef2297dcc67') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== 'a7343bdb0615881e3bf900bfaf42eef2297dcc67') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== 'bba035815ce0298d89d92fbac2312f23f34931e8') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== 'a7343bdb0615881e3bf900bfaf42eef2297dcc67') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
		}
	}
